# Get Accounts

```php
function getAccounts(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null
): Accounts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Accounts array with 0 to n Account

[`Accounts`](../../doc/models/accounts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status==&quot;ACTIVE&quot; AND Type==&quot;BANK&quot;';

$order = 'Name ASC';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getAccounts(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order
    );
    echo 'Accounts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Accounts": [
    {
      "AccountID": "ebd06280-af70-4bed-97c6-7451a454ad85",
      "Code": "091",
      "Name": "Business Savings Account",
      "Type": "BANK",
      "TaxType": "NONE",
      "EnablePaymentsToAccount": false,
      "BankAccountNumber": "0209087654321050",
      "BankAccountType": "BANK",
      "CurrencyCode": "NZD"
    },
    {
      "AccountID": "7d05a53d-613d-4eb2-a2fc-dcb6adb80b80",
      "Code": "200",
      "Name": "Sales",
      "Type": "REVENUE",
      "TaxType": "OUTPUT2",
      "Description": "Income from any normal business activity",
      "EnablePaymentsToAccount": false
    }
  ]
}
```


# Create Account

```php
function createAccount(string $xeroTenantId, Account $body): Accounts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Account`](../../doc/models/account.md) | Body, Required | Account object in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - created new Account and return response of type Accounts array with new Account

[`Accounts`](../../doc/models/accounts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = AccountBuilder::init()
    ->code('123456')
    ->description('Hello World')
    ->name('Foobar')
    ->type(AccountTypeEnum::EXPENSE)
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createAccount(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Accounts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "11814c9d-3b5e-492e-93b0-fad16bf3244f",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550793549392)/",
  "Accounts": [
    {
      "AccountID": "66b262e2-561e-423e-8937-47d558f13442",
      "Code": "123456",
      "Name": "Foobar",
      "Status": "ACTIVE",
      "Type": "EXPENSE",
      "TaxType": "INPUT",
      "Description": "Hello World",
      "Class": "EXPENSE",
      "EnablePaymentsToAccount": false,
      "ShowInExpenseClaims": false,
      "ReportingCode": "EXP",
      "ReportingCodeName": "Expense",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1550793549320+0000)/"
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | Validation Error - some data was incorrect returns response of type Error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Delete Account

```php
function deleteAccount(string $xeroTenantId, string $accountID): Accounts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

# Update Account

```php
function updateAccount(string $xeroTenantId, string $accountID, Accounts $body): Accounts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `accountID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for retrieving single object |
| `body` | [`Accounts`](../../doc/models/accounts.md) | Body, Required | Request of type Accounts array with one Account |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - update existing Account and return response of type Accounts array with updated Account

[`Accounts`](../../doc/models/accounts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$accountID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = AccountsBuilder::init()
    ->accounts(
        [
            AccountBuilder::init()
                ->accountID('99ce6032-0678-4aa0-8148-240c75fee33a')
                ->code('123456')
                ->description('GoodBye World')
                ->enablePaymentsToAccount(false)
                ->name('BarFoo')
                ->reportingCode('EXP')
                ->showInExpenseClaims(false)
                ->taxType('INPUT')
                ->type(AccountTypeEnum::EXPENSE)
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateAccount(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $accountID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Accounts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "9012e75c-ec08-40a9-ae15-153fc1f35c4d",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550795389340)/",
  "Accounts": [
    {
      "AccountID": "99ce6032-0678-4aa0-8148-240c75fee33a",
      "Code": "654321",
      "Name": "BarFoo",
      "Status": "ACTIVE",
      "Type": "EXPENSE",
      "TaxType": "INPUT",
      "Description": "Good Bye World",
      "Class": "EXPENSE",
      "EnablePaymentsToAccount": false,
      "ShowInExpenseClaims": false,
      "ReportingCode": "EXP",
      "ReportingCodeName": "Expense",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1550795389333+0000)/"
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | Validation Error - some data was incorrect returns response of type Error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

# Update Account Attachment by File Name

```php
function updateAccountAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $accountID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `accountID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Account object |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the attachment |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array of Attachment

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

```php
$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateAccountAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $accountID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;

    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Bank Transactions

```php
function getBankTransactions(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?int $page = null,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): BankTransactions
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | Up to 100 bank transactions will be returned in a single API call with line items details |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BankTransactions array with 0 to n BankTransaction

[`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

$order = 'Type ASC';

$page = 1;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getBankTransactions(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        $page,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'BankTransactions:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

# Update or Create Bank Transactions

```php
function updateOrCreateBankTransactions(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    BankTransactions $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): BankTransactions
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BankTransactions array with new BankTransaction

[`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = BankTransactionsBuilder::init()->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateOrCreateBankTransactions(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'BankTransactions:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "5bc1d776-3c7f-4fe8-9b2d-09e747077a88",
```

# Create Bank Transactions

```php
function createBankTransactions(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    BankTransactions $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): BankTransactions
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md) | Body, Required | BankTransactions with an array of BankTransaction objects in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BankTransactions array with new BankTransaction

[`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = BankTransactionsBuilder::init()->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createBankTransactions(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'BankTransactions:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Get Bank Transaction

```php
function getBankTransaction(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $bankTransactionID,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): BankTransactions
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BankTransactions array with a specific BankTransaction

[`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$bankTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getBankTransaction(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $bankTransactionID,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'BankTransactions:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update Bank Transaction

```php
function updateBankTransaction(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $bankTransactionID,
    BankTransactions $body,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): BankTransactions
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |
| `body` | [`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BankTransactions array with updated BankTransaction

[`BankTransactions`](../../doc/models/bank-transactions.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$bankTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = BankTransactionsBuilder::init()->build();

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateBankTransaction(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $bankTransactionID,
        $body,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'BankTransactions:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Bank Transaction Attachments

```php
function getBankTransactionAttachments(string $xeroTenantId, string $bankTransactionID): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with 0 to n Attachment

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$bankTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getBankTransactionAttachments(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $bankTransactionID
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

# Get Bank Transaction Attachment by Id

```php
function getBankTransactionAttachmentById(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $bankTransactionID,
    string $attachmentID,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for an attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for BankTransaction as binary data

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$bankTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$contentType = 'image/jpg';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getBankTransactionAttachmentById(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $bankTransactionID,
        $attachmentID,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update Bank Transaction Attachment by File Name

```php
function updateBankTransactionAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $bankTransactionID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | The name of the file being attached |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of Attachments array of Attachment

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$bankTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$body = FileWrapper::createFromPath('dummy_file');

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateBankTransactionAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $bankTransactionID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json

  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",

    {
      "AttachmentID": "4508a692-e52c-4ad8-a138-2f13e22bf57b",
```

# Create Bank Transaction History Record

```php
function createBankTransactionHistoryRecord(
    string $xeroTenantId,
```

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |

| `bankTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transaction |

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

## Example Usage

```php
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

    $result = $accountingController->createBankTransactionHistoryRecord(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $bankTransactionID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Bank Transfers

```php
function getBankTransfers(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null
): BankTransfers
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of BankTransfers array of 0 to N BankTransfer

[`BankTransfers`](../../doc/models/bank-transfers.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'HasAttachments==true';

$order = 'Amount ASC';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getBankTransfers(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order
    );
    echo 'BankTransfers:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
```

# Create Bank Transfer

```php
function createBankTransfer(string $xeroTenantId, BankTransfers $body): BankTransfers
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`BankTransfers`](../../doc/models/bank-transfers.md) | Body, Required | BankTransfers with array of BankTransfer objects in request body |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of BankTransfers array of one BankTransfer

[`BankTransfers`](../../doc/models/bank-transfers.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = BankTransfersBuilder::init()
    ->bankTransfers(
        [
            BankTransferBuilder::init(
                50,
                AccountBuilder::init()
                    ->accountID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                    ->bankAccountNumber('123455')
                    ->bankAccountType(BankAccountTypeEnum::BANK)
                    ->code('090')
                    ->currencyCode(CurrencyCodeEnum::USD)
                    ->enablePaymentsToAccount(false)
                    ->name('My Savings')
                    ->reportingCode('ASS')
                    ->showInExpenseClaims(false)
                    ->status(StatusEnum::ACTIVE)
                    ->taxType('NONE')
                    ->type(AccountTypeEnum::BANK)
                    ->build(),
                AccountBuilder::init()
                    ->accountID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                    ->bankAccountNumber('123455')
                    ->bankAccountType(BankAccountTypeEnum::BANK)
                    ->code('088')
                    ->currencyCode(CurrencyCodeEnum::USD)
                    ->enablePaymentsToAccount(false)
                    ->name('Business Wells Fargo')
                    ->reportingCode('ASS')
                    ->showInExpenseClaims(false)
                    ->status(StatusEnum::ACTIVE)
                    ->taxType('NONE')
                    ->type(AccountTypeEnum::BANK)
                    ->build()
            )->build()
        ]
    )->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createBankTransfer(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body
    );
    echo 'BankTransfers:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "ae767b68-affd-4e17-bac0-83eaf1854dcd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1551311317475)/",
  "BankTransfers": [
    {
      "BankTransferID": "76eea4b6-f026-464c-b6f3-5fb39a196145",
      "DateString": "2019-02-27T00:00:00",
      "Date": "/Date(1551225600000+0000)/",
      "FromBankAccount": {
        "AccountID": "7e5e243b-9fcd-4aef-8e3a-c70be1e39bfa",
        "Code": "090",
        "Name": "My Savings"
      },
      "ToBankAccount": {
        "AccountID": "6f7594f2-f059-4d56-9e67-47ac9733bfe9",

      },
```

# Get Bank Transfer Attachment by Id

```php
function getBankTransferAttachmentById(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $bankTransferID,
    string $attachmentID,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransferID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transfer |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for an Attachment to a bank transfer |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of binary data from the Attachment to a Bank Transfer

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
    $result = $accountingController->getBankTransferAttachmentById(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $bankTransferID,
        $attachmentID,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `bankTransferID` | `string` | Template, Required | Xero generated unique identifier for a bank transfer |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | The name of the file being attached to a Bank Transfer |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of Attachments array of 0 to N Attachment for a Bank Transfer

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$bankTransferID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$body = FileWrapper::createFromPath('dummy_file');

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateBankTransferAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $bankTransferID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "c7810140-19c2-4ff7-b3ec-b7e95ce7becf",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1551398138226)/",
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "0851935c-c4c5-4de8-9247-ce22efde6f82",
      "FileName": "sample5.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/BankTransfers/6221458a-ef7a-4d5f-9b1c-1b96ce03833c/Attachments/sample5.jpg",
      "MimeType": "image/jpg",
      "ContentLength": 2878711
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

```php
function createBankTransferHistoryRecord(
```

```php
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

    $result = $accountingController->createBankTransferHistoryRecord(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $bankTransferID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
```

# Get Batch Payments

Batch payments allow you to bundle multiple bills or invoices into one payment transaction. This means a single payment in Xero can be reconciled with a single transaction on the bank statement making for a much simpler bank reconciliation experience.

```php
function getBatchPayments(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null
): BatchPayments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BatchPayments array of BatchPayment objects

[`BatchPayments`](../../doc/models/batch-payments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

$order = 'Date ASC';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getBatchPayments(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order
    );
    echo 'BatchPayments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*


# Create Batch Payment

Batch payments allow you to bundle multiple bills or invoices into one payment transaction. This means a single payment in Xero can be reconciled with a single transaction on the bank statement making for a much simpler bank reconciliation experience.

```php
function createBatchPayment(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    BatchPayments $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false
): BatchPayments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`BatchPayments`](../../doc/models/batch-payments.md) | Body, Required | BatchPayments with an array of Payments in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type BatchPayments array of BatchPayment objects

[`BatchPayments`](../../doc/models/batch-payments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = BatchPaymentsBuilder::init()
    ->batchPayments(
        [
            BatchPaymentBuilder::init()
                ->account(
                    AccountBuilder::init()
                        ->accountID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2018-08-01')
                ->payments(
                    [
                        PaymentBuilder::init()
                            ->account(
                                AccountBuilder::init()
                                    ->code('001')
                                    ->build()
                            )
                            ->amount(500)
                            ->date('2019-12-31')
                            ->invoice(
                                InvoiceBuilder::init()
                                    ->contact(
                                        ContactBuilder::init()->build()
                                    )
                                    ->invoiceID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                                    ->lineItems(
                                        []
                                    )
                                    ->type(Type3Enum::ACCPAY)
                                    ->build()
                            )
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->reference('ref')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createBatchPayment(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'BatchPayments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "424745ed-6356-46ad-87d4-3585f9062fb4",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550865988111)/",
  "BatchPayments": [
    {
      "Account": {
        "AccountID": "5ec2f302-cd60-4f8b-a915-9229dd45e6fa"
      },
      "Reference": "Foobar123",
      "BatchPaymentID": "d318c343-208e-49fe-b04a-45642349bcf1",

        {
          "Invoice": {
```

# Create Branding Theme Payment Services

```php
function createBrandingThemePaymentServices(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $brandingThemeID,
    PaymentService $body
): PaymentServices
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `brandingThemeID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Branding Theme |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`paymentservices`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type PaymentServices array with newly created PaymentService

[`PaymentServices`](../../doc/models/payment-services.md)

## Example Usage

```php

    ->payNowText('Pay Now')
    ->paymentServiceID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
    ->paymentServiceName('ACME Payments')
    ->paymentServiceUrl('https://www.payupnow.com/')
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createBrandingThemePaymentServices(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $brandingThemeID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'PaymentServices:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "918feecb-067a-4ed9-841b-571c04eaada3",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1551139338915)/",
  "PaymentServices": [
    {
      "PaymentServiceID": "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
```

# Get Contacts

```php
function getContacts(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?array $iDs = null,
    ?int $page = null,
    ?bool $includeArchived = null
): Contacts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `iDs` | `?(string[])` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma separated list of ContactIDs. Allows you to retrieve a specific set of contacts in a single call. |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 - Up to 100 contacts will be returned in a single API call. |
| `includeArchived` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | e.g. includeArchived=true - Contacts with a status of ARCHIVED will be included in the response |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.contacts.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Contacts array with 0 to N Contact

[`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'ContactStatus==&quot;ACTIVE&quot;';

$order = 'Name ASC';

$page = 1;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getContacts(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        null,
        $page
    );
    echo 'Contacts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update or Create Contacts

```php
function updateOrCreateContacts(string $xeroTenantId, Contacts $body, ?bool $summarizeErrors = false): Contacts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.contacts`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Contacts array with newly created Contact

[`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = ContactsBuilder::init()
    ->contacts(
        [
            ContactBuilder::init()
                ->emailAddress('hulk@avengers.com')
                ->name('Bruce Banner')
                ->paymentTerms(
                    PaymentTermBuilder::init()
                        ->bills(
                            BillBuilder::init()
                                ->day(15)
                                ->type(PaymentTermTypeEnum::OFCURRENTMONTH)
                                ->build()
                        )
                        ->sales(
                            BillBuilder::init()
                                ->day(10)
                                ->type(PaymentTermTypeEnum::DAYSAFTERBILLMONTH)
                                ->build()
                        )
                        ->build()
                )
                ->phones(
                    [
                        PhoneBuilder::init()
                            ->phoneAreaCode('415')
                            ->phoneNumber('555-1212')
                            ->phoneType(PhoneTypeEnum::MOBILE)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateOrCreateContacts(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'Contacts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "e997d6d7-6dad-4458-beb8-d9c1bf7f2edf",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1551399321121)/",
  "Contacts": [
    {
      "ContactID": "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000",
      "ContactStatus": "ACTIVE",
      "Name": "Bruce Banner",
      "EmailAddress": "bruce@banner.com",
      "BankAccountDetails": "",
      "Addresses": [
        {
          "AddressType": "STREET",
          "City": "",

          "AddressType": "POBOX",
          "City": "",
          "Region": "",
          "PostalCode": "",

          "PhoneType": "DEFAULT",
```

# Create Contacts

```php
function createContacts(string $xeroTenantId, Contacts $body, ?bool $summarizeErrors = false): Contacts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md) | Body, Required | Contacts with an array of Contact objects to create in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.contacts`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Contacts array with newly created Contact

[`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = ContactsBuilder::init()
    ->contacts(
        [
            ContactBuilder::init()
                ->addresses(
                    [
                        AddressBuilder::init()
                            ->addressType(AddressTypeEnum::STREET)
                            ->city('')
                            ->country('')
                            ->postalCode('')
                            ->region('')
                            ->build(),
                        AddressBuilder::init()
                            ->addressType(AddressTypeEnum::POBOX)
                            ->city('')
                            ->country('')
                            ->postalCode('')
                            ->region('')
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->bankAccountDetails('')
                ->contactGroups(
                    []
                )
                ->contactID('3ff6d40c-af9a-40a3-89ce-3c1556a25591')
                ->contactPersons(
                    []
                )
                ->contactStatus(ContactStatusEnum::ACTIVE)
                ->emailAddress('sid32476@blah.com')
                ->hasValidationErrors(false)
                ->isCustomer(false)
                ->isSupplier(false)
                ->name('Foo9987')
                ->paymentTerms(
                    PaymentTermBuilder::init()
                        ->bills(
                            BillBuilder::init()
                                ->day(15)
                                ->type(PaymentTermTypeEnum::OFCURRENTMONTH)
                                ->build()
                        )
                        ->sales(
                            BillBuilder::init()
                                ->day(10)
                                ->type(PaymentTermTypeEnum::DAYSAFTERBILLMONTH)
                                ->build()
                        )
                        ->build()
                )
                ->phones(
                    [
                        PhoneBuilder::init()
                            ->phoneAreaCode('')
                            ->phoneCountryCode('')
                            ->phoneNumber('')
                            ->phoneType(PhoneTypeEnum::DEFAULT_)
                            ->build(),
                        PhoneBuilder::init()
                            ->phoneAreaCode('')
                            ->phoneCountryCode('')
                            ->phoneNumber('')
                            ->phoneType(PhoneTypeEnum::DDI)
                            ->build(),
                        PhoneBuilder::init()
                            ->phoneAreaCode('')
                            ->phoneCountryCode('')
                            ->phoneNumber('')
                            ->phoneType(PhoneTypeEnum::FAX)
                            ->build(),
                        PhoneBuilder::init()
                            ->phoneAreaCode('415')
                            ->phoneCountryCode('')
                            ->phoneNumber('555-1212')
                            ->phoneType(PhoneTypeEnum::MOBILE)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->purchasesTrackingCategories(
                    []
                )
                ->salesTrackingCategories(
                    []
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createContacts(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'Contacts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update Contact

```php
function updateContact(string $xeroTenantId, string $contactID, Contacts $body): Contacts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `contactID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Contact |
| `body` | [`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md) | Body, Required | an array of Contacts containing single Contact object with properties to update |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.contacts`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Contacts array with an updated Contact

[`Contacts`](../../doc/models/contacts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = ContactsBuilder::init()
    ->contacts(
        [
            ContactBuilder::init()
                ->contactID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                ->name('Thanos')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateContact(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $contactID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Contacts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Contact Attachment by Id

```php
function getContactAttachmentById(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $contactID,
    string $attachmentID,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `contactID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Contact |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Contact as binary data

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$contentType = 'image/jpg';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getContactAttachmentById(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $contactID,
        $attachmentID,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Get Contact Attachment by File Name

```php
function getContactAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $contactID,
    string $fileName,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `contactID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Contact |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name for the file you are attaching |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Contact as binary data

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$contentType = 'image/jpg';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getContactAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $contactID,
        $fileName,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Update Contact Attachment by File Name

```php
function updateContactAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $contactID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `contactID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Contact |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name for the file you are attaching |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with an updated Attachment

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$body = FileWrapper::createFromPath('dummy_file');

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateContactAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $contactID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "8543ae1a-297c-49b8-bf91-47decac452d5",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1551485146555)/",
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "8b537c1b-bbb5-47fd-857e-370c369dda7c",
      "FileName": "HelloWorld.jpg",

      "MimeType": "image/jpg",
      "ContentLength": 2878711
    }
  ]
}
```

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

# Create Contact History

```php
function createContactHistory(string $xeroTenantId, string $contactID, HistoryRecords $body): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `contactID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Contact |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.contacts`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createContactHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $contactID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

```php
function getContactByContactNumber(string $xeroTenantId, string $contactNumber): Contacts
```

# Get Credit Notes

```php
function getCreditNotes(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?int $page = null,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): CreditNotes
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 credit notes will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each credit note |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Credit Notes array of CreditNote

[`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="DRAFT"';

$order = 'CreditNoteNumber ASC';

$page = 1;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getCreditNotes(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        $page,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'CreditNotes:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
```

# Update or Create Credit Notes

```php
function updateOrCreateCreditNotes(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    CreditNotes $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): CreditNotes
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md) | Body, Required | an array of Credit Notes with a single CreditNote object. |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Credit Notes array of newly created CreditNote

[`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = CreditNotesBuilder::init()
    ->creditNotes(
        [
            CreditNoteBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2019-01-05')
                ->lineItems(
                    [
                        LineItemBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('400')
                            ->description('Foobar')
                            ->quantity(2)
                            ->unitAmount(20)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->reference('HelloWorld')
                ->status(Status7Enum::AUTHORISED)
                ->type(Type4Enum::ACCPAYCREDIT)
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateOrCreateCreditNotes(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'CreditNotes:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "5e57a661-42da-4a19-96a0-00405a0e946d",

    {
      "CreditNoteID": "f9256f04-5a99-4680-acb9-6b4639cc439a",

      "Payments": [],

        "ContactID": "430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8",
```

# Create Credit Notes

```php
function createCreditNotes(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    CreditNotes $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): CreditNotes
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md) | Body, Required | Credit Notes with array of CreditNote object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Credit Notes array of newly created CreditNote

[`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = CreditNotesBuilder::init()
    ->creditNotes(
        [
            CreditNoteBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2019-01-05')
                ->lineItems(
                    [
                        LineItemBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('400')
                            ->description('Foobar')
                            ->quantity(2)
                            ->unitAmount(20)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->type(Type4Enum::ACCPAYCREDIT)
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createCreditNotes(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'CreditNotes:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Credit Note

```php
function getCreditNote(string $xeroTenantId, string $creditNoteID, ?int $unitdp = null): CreditNotes
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

# Update Credit Note

```php
function updateCreditNote(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $creditNoteID,
    CreditNotes $body,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): CreditNotes
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `body` | [`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md) | Body, Required | an array of Credit Notes containing credit note details to update |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Credit Notes array with updated CreditNote

[`CreditNotes`](../../doc/models/credit-notes.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$creditNoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = CreditNotesBuilder::init()
    ->creditNotes(
        [
            CreditNoteBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2019-01-05')
                ->lineItems(
                    [
                        LineItemBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('400')
                            ->description('Foobar')
                            ->quantity(2)
                            ->unitAmount(20)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->reference('HelloWorld')
                ->status(Status7Enum::AUTHORISED)
                ->type(Type4Enum::ACCPAYCREDIT)
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateCreditNote(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $creditNoteID,
        $body,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'CreditNotes:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Create Credit Note Allocation

```php
function createCreditNoteAllocation(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $creditNoteID,
    Allocations $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false
): Allocations
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `body` | [`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md) | Body, Required | Allocations with array of Allocation object in body of request. |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Allocations array with newly created Allocation for specific Credit Note

[`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$creditNoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = AllocationsBuilder::init()
    ->allocations(
        [
            AllocationBuilder::init(
                1,
                '2019-03-05',
                InvoiceBuilder::init()
                    ->invoiceID('c45720a1-ade3-4a38-a064-d15489be6841')
                    ->lineItems(
                        []
                    )
                    ->build()
            )->build()
        ]
    )->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createCreditNoteAllocation(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $creditNoteID,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'Allocations:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Credit Note Attachment by Id

```php
function getCreditNoteAttachmentById(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $creditNoteID,
    string $attachmentID,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Credit Note as binary data

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$creditNoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$contentType = 'image/jpg';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getCreditNoteAttachmentById(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $creditNoteID,
        $attachmentID,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Get Credit Note Attachment by File Name

```php
): string
```

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |

### OAuth2

## Response Type

```php
        $xeroTenantId,

        $contentType
    );

} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update Credit Note Attachment by File Name

```php
function updateCreditNoteAttachmentByFileName(

    string $creditNoteID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |

| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |

| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

```php
    $result = $accountingController->updateCreditNoteAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $creditNoteID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Create Credit Note Attachment by File Name

```php
function createCreditNoteAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $creditNoteID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body,
    ?bool $includeOnline = false
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the file you are attaching to Credit Note |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `includeOnline` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | Allows an attachment to be seen by the end customer within their online invoice<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with newly created Attachment for specific Credit Note

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$creditNoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$body = FileWrapper::createFromPath('dummy_file');

$includeOnline = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createCreditNoteAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $creditNoteID,
        $fileName,
        $body,
        $includeOnline
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "22a8d402-5dea-40ed-9d01-26896429f649",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1551822953320)/",
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "91bbae3f-5de5-4e3d-875f-8662f25897bd",
      "FileName": "sample5.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/CreditNotes/249f15fa-f2a7-4acc-8769-0984103f2225/Attachments/sample5.jpg",
      "MimeType": "image/jpg",
      "ContentLength": 2878711
    }
  ]
```

# Create Credit Note History

```php
function createCreditNoteHistory(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $creditNoteID,
    HistoryRecords $body
): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `creditNoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Credit Note |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$creditNoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createCreditNoteHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $creditNoteID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

# Get Employees

```php
function getEmployees(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null
): Employees
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Employees array with all Employee

[`Employees`](../../doc/models/employees.md)

```php
$order = 'LastName ASC';

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getEmployees(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order
    );

    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update or Create Employees

```php
function updateOrCreateEmployees(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    Employees $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false
): Employees
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Employees`](../../doc/models/employees.md) | Body, Required | Employees with array of Employee object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Employees array with new Employee

[`Employees`](../../doc/models/employees.md)

## Example Usage

```php

    ->employees(
        [
            EmployeeBuilder::init()
                ->externalLink(
                    ExternalLinkBuilder::init()
                        ->url('http://twitter.com/#!/search/Nick+Fury')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->firstName('Nick')
                ->lastName('Fury')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateOrCreateEmployees(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'Employees:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "0d6a08e7-6936-4828-a1bc-e4595e0ef778",
```
