# Get Expense Claims

```php
function getExpenseClaims(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null
): ExpenseClaims
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ExpenseClaims array with all ExpenseClaims

[`ExpenseClaims`](../../doc/models/expense-claims.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="SUBMITTED"';

$order = 'Status ASC';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getExpenseClaims(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order
    );
    echo 'ExpenseClaims:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "f6a8867e-af29-41ee-8f77-855f5ff214fe",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552325853538)/",
  "ExpenseClaims": [
    {
      "ExpenseClaimID": "646b15ab-b874-4e13-82ae-f4385b2ac4b6",
      "Status": "AUTHORISED",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552325851767+0000)/",
      "User": {
        "UserID": "d1164823-0ac1-41ad-987b-b4e30fe0b273",
        "EmailAddress": "api@xero.com",
        "FirstName": "API ",
        "LastName": "Team",
        "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1511957179217+0000)/",
        "IsSubscriber": true,
        "OrganisationRole": "FINANCIALADVISER"
      },
      "Receipts": [],
      "Payments": [],
      "Total": 40.0,
      "AmountDue": 40.0,
      "AmountPaid": 0.0,
      "ReportingDate": "/Date(1552262400000+0000)/"
    }
  ]
}
```

# Create Expense Claims

```php
function createExpenseClaims(string $xeroTenantId, ExpenseClaims $body): ExpenseClaims
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`ExpenseClaims`](../../doc/models/expense-claims.md) | Body, Required | ExpenseClaims with array of ExpenseClaim object in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ExpenseClaims array with newly created ExpenseClaim

[`ExpenseClaims`](../../doc/models/expense-claims.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = ExpenseClaimsBuilder::init()
    ->expenseClaims(
        [
            ExpenseClaimBuilder::init()
                ->receipts(
                    [
                        ReceiptBuilder::init()
                            ->receiptID('dc1c7f6d-0a4c-402f-acac-551d62ce5816')
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->status(Status12Enum::SUBMITTED)
                ->user(
                    UserBuilder::init()
                        ->userID('d1164823-0ac1-41ad-987b-b4e30fe0b273')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createExpenseClaims(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body
    );
    echo 'ExpenseClaims:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*


# Update Expense Claim

```php
function updateExpenseClaim(string $xeroTenantId, string $expenseClaimID, ExpenseClaims $body): ExpenseClaims
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `expenseClaimID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a ExpenseClaim |
| `body` | [`ExpenseClaims`](../../doc/models/expense-claims.md) | Body, Required | - |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ExpenseClaims array with updated ExpenseClaim

[`ExpenseClaims`](../../doc/models/expense-claims.md)

## Example Usage

```php
                        ReceiptBuilder::init()

                        ->build()
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateExpenseClaim(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $expenseClaimID,
        $body
    );
```

# Create Expense Claim History

```php
function createExpenseClaimHistory(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $expenseClaimID,
    HistoryRecords $body
): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `expenseClaimID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a ExpenseClaim |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$expenseClaimID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createExpenseClaimHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $expenseClaimID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
```

# Get Invoices

```php
function getInvoices(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?array $iDs = null,
    ?array $invoiceNumbers = null,
    ?array $contactIDs = null,
    ?array $statuses = null,
    ?int $page = null,
    ?bool $includeArchived = null,
    ?bool $createdByMyApp = null,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): Invoices
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `iDs` | `?(string[])` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma-separated list of InvoicesIDs. |
| `invoiceNumbers` | `?(string[])` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma-separated list of InvoiceNumbers. |
| `contactIDs` | `?(string[])` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma-separated list of ContactIDs. |
| `statuses` | `?(string[])` | Query, Optional | Filter by a comma-separated list Statuses. For faster response times we recommend using these explicit parameters instead of passing OR conditions into the Where filter. |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 invoices will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each invoice |
| `includeArchived` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | e.g. includeArchived=true - Contacts with a status of ARCHIVED will be included in the response |
| `createdByMyApp` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | When set to true you'll only retrieve Invoices created by your app |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with all Invoices

[`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="DRAFT"';

$order = 'InvoiceNumber ASC';

$page = 1;

$createdByMyApp = false;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getInvoices(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        $page,
        null,
        $createdByMyApp,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Invoices:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update or Create Invoices

```php
function updateOrCreateInvoices(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    Invoices $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): Invoices
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with newly created Invoice

[`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = InvoicesBuilder::init()
    ->invoices(
        [
            InvoiceBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2019-03-11')
                ->dueDate('2018-12-10')
                ->lineItems(
                    [
                        LineItemBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('200')
                            ->description('Acme Tires')
                            ->lineAmount(40)
                            ->quantity(2)
                            ->taxType('NONE')
                            ->unitAmount(20)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->reference('Website Design')
                ->status(Status5Enum::AUTHORISED)
                ->type(Type3Enum::ACCREC)
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateOrCreateInvoices(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Invoices:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*


# Create Invoices

```php
function createInvoices(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    Invoices $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): Invoices
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md) | Body, Required | Invoices with an array of invoice objects in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with newly created Invoice

[`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = InvoicesBuilder::init()
    ->invoices(
        [
            InvoiceBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2019-03-11')
                ->dueDate('2018-12-10')
                ->lineItems(
                    [
                        LineItemBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('200')
                            ->description('Acme Tires')
                            ->lineAmount(40)
                            ->quantity(2)
                            ->taxType('NONE')
                            ->unitAmount(20)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->reference('Website Design')
                ->status(Status5Enum::AUTHORISED)
                ->type(Type3Enum::ACCREC)
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createInvoices(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Invoices:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Invoice

```php
function getInvoice(string $xeroTenantId, string $invoiceID, ?int $unitdp = null): Invoices
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with specified Invoices

[`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getInvoice(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Invoices:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update Invoice

```php
function updateInvoice(string $xeroTenantId, string $invoiceID, Invoices $body, ?int $unitdp = null): Invoices
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `body` | [`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Invoices array with updated Invoice

[`Invoices`](../../doc/models/invoices.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = InvoicesBuilder::init()
    ->invoices(
        [
            InvoiceBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()->build()
                )
                ->invoiceID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                ->lineItems(
                    []
                )
                ->reference('May the force be with you')
                ->type(Type3Enum::ACCPAY)
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateInvoice(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID,
        $body,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Invoices:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Get Invoice Attachments

```php
function getInvoiceAttachments(string $xeroTenantId, string $invoiceID): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array of Attachments for specified Invoices

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getInvoiceAttachments(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "7e357a45-69f5-4e8f-8d7b-15da8ef50aab",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552330258523)/",
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "9808ad7f-c8d4-41cf-995e-bc29cb76fd2c",
      "FileName": "foobar.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/Invoices/4074292c-09b3-456d-84e7-add864c6c39b/Attachments/foobar.jpg",
      "MimeType": "image/jpg",
      "ContentLength": 2878711
    },
    {
      "AttachmentID": "5a500c1a-5a02-48de-939e-1d234fd170d4",
      "FileName": "sample5.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/Invoices/4074292c-09b3-456d-84e7-add864c6c39b/Attachments/sample5.jpg",
      "MimeType": "image/jpg",
      "ContentLength": 2878711
    }
  ]
}
```


# Get Invoice Attachment by Id

```php
function getInvoiceAttachmentById(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $invoiceID,
    string $attachmentID,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Invoice as binary data

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$contentType = 'image/jpg';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getInvoiceAttachmentById(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID,
        $attachmentID,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Get Invoice Attachment by File Name

```php
function getInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $invoiceID,
    string $fileName,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the file you are attaching |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Invoice as binary data

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$contentType = 'image/jpg';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID,
        $fileName,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Update Invoice Attachment by File Name

```php
function updateInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $invoiceID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the file you are attaching |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with updated Attachment

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$body = FileWrapper::createFromPath('dummy_file');

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "acd7d618-5fef-4d45-849c-a339ea31a973",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552330524005)/",
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "08085449-fda3-45f4-a685-ff44c8a29ee3",
      "FileName": "HelloWorld.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/Invoices/4074292c-09b3-456d-84e7-add864c6c39b/Attachments/HelloWorld.jpg",
      "MimeType": "image/jpg",
      "ContentLength": 2878711
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Create Invoice Attachment by File Name

```php
function createInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $invoiceID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body,
    ?bool $includeOnline = false
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the file you are attaching |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |
| `includeOnline` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | Allows an attachment to be seen by the end customer within their online invoice<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with newly created Attachment

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$body = FileWrapper::createFromPath('dummy_file');

$includeOnline = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID,
        $fileName,
        $body,
        $includeOnline
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "971fbd18-c850-453a-825f-63f2fee096ee",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552330001318)/",
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "5a500c1a-5a02-48de-939e-1d234fd170d4",
      "FileName": "sample5.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/Invoices/4074292c-09b3-456d-84e7-add864c6c39b/Attachments/sample5.jpg",
      "MimeType": "image/jpg",
      "ContentLength": 2878711
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Email Invoice

```php
function emailInvoice(string $xeroTenantId, string $invoiceID, RequestEmpty $body): void
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `body` | [`RequestEmpty`](../../doc/models/request-empty.md) | Body, Required | - |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**204**: Success - return response 204 no content

`void`

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = RequestEmptyBuilder::init()->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $accountingController->emailInvoice(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID,
        $body
    );
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Get Invoice History

```php
function getInvoiceHistory(string $xeroTenantId, string $invoiceID): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of HistoryRecords array of 0 to N HistoryRecord

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getInvoiceHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Create Invoice History

```php
function createInvoiceHistory(string $xeroTenantId, string $invoiceID, HistoryRecords $body): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `invoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Invoice |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$invoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createInvoiceHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $invoiceID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

# Get Items

```php
function getItems(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): Items
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Items array with all Item

[`Items`](../../doc/models/items.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'IsSold==true';

$order = 'Code ASC';

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getItems(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Items:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update or Create Items

```php
function updateOrCreateItems(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    Items $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): Items
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Items`](../../doc/models/items.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Items array with newly created Item

[`Items`](../../doc/models/items.md)

## Example Usage

```php
    ->items(
        [
            ItemBuilder::init(
                'ItemCode123'
            )

                ->name('ItemName XYZ')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

    $result = $accountingController->updateOrCreateItems(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Items:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

| `body` | [`Items`](../../doc/models/items.md) | Body, Required | Items with an array of Item objects in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

# Get Journals

```php
function getJournals(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?int $offset = null,
    ?bool $paymentsOnly = null
): Journals
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `offset` | `?int` | Query, Optional | Offset by a specified journal number. e.g. journals with a JournalNumber greater than the offset will be returned |
| `paymentsOnly` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | Filter to retrieve journals on a cash basis. Journals are returned on an accrual basis by default. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.journals.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Journals array with all Journals

[`Journals`](../../doc/models/journals.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$offset = 10;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getJournals(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $offset
    );
    echo 'Journals:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Linked Transactions

```php
function getLinkedTransactions(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?int $page = null,
    ?string $linkedTransactionID = null,
    ?string $sourceTransactionID = null,
    ?string $contactID = null,
    ?string $status = null,
    ?string $targetTransactionID = null
): LinkedTransactions
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | Up to 100 linked transactions will be returned in a single API call. Use the page parameter to specify the page to be returned e.g. page=1. |
| `linkedTransactionID` | `?string` | Query, Optional | The Xero identifier for an Linked Transaction |
| `sourceTransactionID` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by the SourceTransactionID. Get the linked transactions created from a particular ACCPAY invoice |
| `contactID` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by the ContactID. Get all the linked transactions that have been assigned to a particular customer. |
| `status` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by the combination of ContactID and Status. Get  the linked transactions associated to a  customer and with a status |
| `targetTransactionID` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by the TargetTransactionID. Get all the linked transactions allocated to a particular ACCREC invoice |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type LinkedTransactions array with all LinkedTransaction

[`LinkedTransactions`](../../doc/models/linked-transactions.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$page = 1;

$linkedTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$sourceTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$status = 'APPROVED';

$targetTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getLinkedTransactions(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $page,
        $linkedTransactionID,
        $sourceTransactionID,
        $contactID,
        $status,
        $targetTransactionID
    );
    echo 'LinkedTransactions:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "516aabd0-e670-48d5-b0eb-10dce4494dd8",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552348338096)/",
  "LinkedTransactions": [
    {
      "LinkedTransactionID": "5cf7d9c0-b9a7-4433-a2dc-ae3c11bba39b",
      "SourceTransactionID": "aec416dd-38ea-40dc-9f0b-813c8c71f87f",
      "SourceLineItemID": "77e0b23b-5b79-4f4b-ae20-c9031d41442f",
      "ContactID": "430fa14a-f945-44d3-9f97-5df5e28441b8",
      "TargetTransactionID": "83693fc1-5b05-4807-b190-109d4a85dd5f",
      "TargetLineItemID": "d5128ff1-0f39-4d2a-a6d5-46dfaf5f075c",
      "Status": "ONDRAFT",
      "Type": "BILLABLEEXPENSE",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552347991000+0000)/",
      "SourceTransactionTypeCode": "ACCPAY"
    }
  ]
}
```


# Create Linked Transaction

```php
function createLinkedTransaction(string $xeroTenantId, LinkedTransaction $body): LinkedTransactions
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`LinkedTransaction`](../../doc/models/linked-transaction.md) | Body, Required | LinkedTransaction object in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type LinkedTransactions array with newly created LinkedTransaction

[`LinkedTransactions`](../../doc/models/linked-transactions.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = LinkedTransactionBuilder::init()->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createLinkedTransaction(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body
    );
    echo 'LinkedTransactions:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "f32b30e5-32d1-42a8-bcc9-5b22828f725c",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552351054646)/",
  "LinkedTransactions": [
    {
      "LinkedTransactionID": "e9684b6c-4df9-45a0-917b-85cc29857008",
      "SourceTransactionID": "a848644a-f20f-4630-98c3-386bd7505631",
      "SourceLineItemID": "b0df260d-3cc8-4ced-9bd6-41924f624ed3",
      "Status": "DRAFT",
      "Type": "BILLABLEEXPENSE",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552351055000+0000)/",
      "SourceTransactionTypeCode": "ACCPAY",
      "ValidationErrors": [
        {
          "Message": "The SourceLineItemID and SourceTransactionID do not match"
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

# Update Linked Transaction

```php
function updateLinkedTransaction(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $linkedTransactionID,
    LinkedTransactions $body
): LinkedTransactions
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `linkedTransactionID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a LinkedTransaction |
| `body` | [`LinkedTransactions`](../../doc/models/linked-transactions.md) | Body, Required | - |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type LinkedTransactions array with updated LinkedTransaction

[`LinkedTransactions`](../../doc/models/linked-transactions.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$linkedTransactionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = LinkedTransactionsBuilder::init()
    ->linkedTransactions(
        [
            LinkedTransactionBuilder::init()
                ->sourceLineItemID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                ->sourceTransactionID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateLinkedTransaction(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $linkedTransactionID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'LinkedTransactions:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "bd364af7-08f0-432b-81db-c1e5ba05f3dd",
  "Status": "OK",

  "LinkedTransactions": [
    {
      "LinkedTransactionID": "e9684b6c-4df9-45a0-917b-85cc29857008",

      "Status": "DRAFT",
      "Type": "BILLABLEEXPENSE",
```

# Get Manual Journals

```php
function getManualJournals(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?int $page = null
): ManualJournals
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 manual journals will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each overpayment |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ManualJournals array with a all ManualJournals

[`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="DRAFT"';

$order = 'Date ASC';

$page = 1;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getManualJournals(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        $page
    );
    echo 'ManualJournals:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "8a508ec1-b578-48bf-97df-020c918fbf7d",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",

      "JournalLines": [],
      "ShowOnCashBasisReports": true,
      "HasAttachments": false
    },
    {
      "Date": "/Date(1552348800000+0000)/",
      "Status": "POSTED",
      "LineAmountTypes": "NoTax",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552357188147+0000)/",
      "ManualJournalID": "99cb8353-ce73-4a5d-8e0d-8b0edf86cfc4",

      "JournalLines": [],
```

# Update or Create Manual Journals

```php
function updateOrCreateManualJournals(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ManualJournals $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false
): ManualJournals
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md) | Body, Required | ManualJournals array with ManualJournal object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ManualJournals array with newly created ManualJournal

[`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = ManualJournalsBuilder::init()
    ->manualJournals(
        [
            ManualJournalBuilder::init(
                'Journal Desc'
            )
                ->date('2019-03-14')
                ->journalLines(
                    [
                        ManualJournalLineBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('400')
                            ->description('Money Movement')
                            ->lineAmount(100)
                            ->build(),
                        ManualJournalLineBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('400')
                            ->description('Prepayment of things')
                            ->lineAmount(-100)
                            ->tracking(
                                [
                                    TrackingCategoryBuilder::init()
                                        ->name('North')
                                        ->option('Region')
                                        ->build()
                                ]
                            )
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateOrCreateManualJournals(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'ManualJournals:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "45dfa608-0fcb-4f30-a377-c82cd348569c",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552595972952)/",
  "ManualJournals": [
    {
      "Date": "/Date(1552521600000+0000)/",
      "Status": "DRAFT",
      "LineAmountTypes": "NoTax",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552595972920+0000)/",
      "ManualJournalID": "d312dd5e-a53e-46d1-9d51-c569ef4570b7",
      "Narration": "Foo bar",
      "JournalLines": [
        {
          "Description": "Hello there",
          "TaxType": "NONE",
          "LineAmount": 100.0,
          "AccountCode": "400",
          "Tracking": [],
          "AccountID": "c4f29c22-28c2-4a13-9eab-ecbbd641ffdf",
          "IsBlank": false
        },
        {
          "Description": "Goodbye",
          "TaxType": "NONE",
          "LineAmount": -100.0,
          "AccountCode": "400",
          "Tracking": [
            {
              "Name": "Simpsons",

```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Create Manual Journals

```php
function createManualJournals(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ManualJournals $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false
): ManualJournals
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md) | Body, Required | ManualJournals array with ManualJournal object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ManualJournals array with newly created ManualJournal

[`ManualJournals`](../../doc/models/manual-journals.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = ManualJournalsBuilder::init()
    ->manualJournals(
        [
            ManualJournalBuilder::init(
                'Journal Desc'
            )
                ->date('2019-03-14')
                ->journalLines(
                    [
                        ManualJournalLineBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('400')
                            ->description('Money Movement')
                            ->lineAmount(100)
                            ->build(),
                        ManualJournalLineBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('400')
                            ->description('Prepayment of things')
                            ->lineAmount(-100)
                            ->tracking(
                                [
                                    TrackingCategoryBuilder::init()
                                        ->name('North')
                                        ->option('Region')
                                        ->build()
                                ]
                            )
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createManualJournals(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'ManualJournals:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "45dfa608-0fcb-4f30-a377-c82cd348569c",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552595972952)/",
  "ManualJournals": [
    {
      "Date": "/Date(1552521600000+0000)/",
      "Status": "DRAFT",
      "LineAmountTypes": "NoTax",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1552595972920+0000)/",
```

```php
    string $xeroTenantId,
```

## Authentication

### OAuth2

`string`

```php
    $result = $accountingController->getManualJournalAttachmentById(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $manualJournalID,
        $attachmentID,
        $contentType
    );

    var_dump($result);

    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$manualJournalID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createManualJournalHistoryRecord(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $manualJournalID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

# Get Overpayments

```php
function getOverpayments(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?int $page = null,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): Overpayments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 overpayments will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each overpayment |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Overpayments array with all Overpayments

[`Overpayments`](../../doc/models/overpayments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

$order = 'Status ASC';

$page = 1;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getOverpayments(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        $page,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Overpayments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Create Overpayment Allocations

```php
function createOverpaymentAllocations(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $overpaymentID,
    Allocations $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false
): Allocations
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `overpaymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Overpayment |
| `body` | [`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md) | Body, Required | Allocations array with Allocation object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Allocations array with all Allocation for Overpayments

[`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$overpaymentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = AllocationsBuilder::init()
    ->allocations(
        [
            AllocationBuilder::init(
                10,
                '2019-03-12',
                InvoiceBuilder::init()
                    ->contact(
                        ContactBuilder::init()->build()
                    )
                    ->invoiceID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                    ->lineItems(
                        []
                    )
                    ->type(Type3Enum::ACCPAY)
                    ->build()
            )->build()
        ]
    )->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createOverpaymentAllocations(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $overpaymentID,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'Allocations:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "3b7f7be2-384a-4703-bcfb-c56e9116c914",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552428952968)/",
  "Allocations": [
    {
      "Amount": 1.0,
      "Date": "/Date(1552348800000+0000)/",
      "Invoice": {
        "InvoiceID": "c45720a1-ade3-4a38-a064-d15489be6841",
        "Payments": [],
        "CreditNotes": [],
        "Prepayments": [],
        "Overpayments": [],
        "HasErrors": false,
        "IsDiscounted": false,
        "LineItems": [],
        "ValidationErrors": []
      },
      "Overpayment": {
        "OverpaymentID": "ed7f6041-c915-4667-bd1d-54c48e92161e",
        "ID": "ed7f6041-c915-4667-bd1d-54c48e92161e",
        "LineItems": []
      },
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Get Overpayment History

```php
function getOverpaymentHistory(string $xeroTenantId, string $overpaymentID): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `overpaymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Overpayment |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of HistoryRecords array of 0 to N HistoryRecord

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$overpaymentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getOverpaymentHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $overpaymentID
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
```

# Create Overpayment History

```php
function createOverpaymentHistory(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $overpaymentID,
    HistoryRecords $body
): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `overpaymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Overpayment |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$overpaymentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createOverpaymentHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $overpaymentID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error - API is not able to create HistoryRecord for Overpayments | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

# Create Payment Service

```php
function createPaymentService(string $xeroTenantId, PaymentServices $body): PaymentServices
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`PaymentServices`](../../doc/models/payment-services.md) | Body, Required | PaymentServices array with PaymentService object in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`paymentservices`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type PaymentServices array for newly created PaymentService

[`PaymentServices`](../../doc/models/payment-services.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = PaymentServicesBuilder::init()
    ->paymentServices(
        [
            PaymentServiceBuilder::init()
                ->payNowText('Time To Pay')
                ->paymentServiceName('PayUpNow')
                ->paymentServiceUrl('https://www.payupnow.com/')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createPaymentService(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body
    );
    echo 'PaymentServices:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "7ed8b3c0-2155-49ee-a583-f2dce6607dfb",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552488712813)/",
  "PaymentServices": [
    {
      "PaymentServiceID": "54b3b4f6-0443-4fba-bcd1-61ec0c35ca55",
      "PaymentServiceName": "PayUpNow",
      "PaymentServiceUrl": "https://www.payupnow.com/",
      "PaymentServiceType": "Custom",
      "PayNowText": "Time To Pay",
      "ValidationErrors": [
        {
          "Message": "Payment service could not be found"
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Get Payments

```php
function getPayments(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?int $page = null
): Payments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | Up to 100 payments will be returned in a single API call |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Payments array for all Payments

[`Payments`](../../doc/models/payments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

$order = 'Amount ASC';

$page = 1;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getPayments(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        $page
    );
    echo 'Payments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
```

# Create Payments

```php
function createPayments(string $xeroTenantId, Payments $body, ?bool $summarizeErrors = false): Payments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Payments`](../../doc/models/payments.md) | Body, Required | Payments array with Payment object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Payments array for newly created Payment

[`Payments`](../../doc/models/payments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = PaymentsBuilder::init()
    ->payments(
        [
            PaymentBuilder::init()
                ->account(
                    AccountBuilder::init()
                        ->code('970')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->amount(1)
                ->date('2019-03-12')
                ->invoice(
                    InvoiceBuilder::init()
                        ->invoiceID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                        ->lineItems(
                            []
                        )
                        ->build()
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createPayments(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'Payments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*


# Delete Payment

```php
function deletePayment(string $xeroTenantId, string $paymentID, PaymentDelete $body): Payments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `paymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Payment |
| `body` | [`PaymentDelete`](../../doc/models/payment-delete.md) | Body, Required | - |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Payments array for updated Payment

[`Payments`](../../doc/models/payments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$paymentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = PaymentDeleteBuilder::init(
    'DELETED'
)->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->deletePayment(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $paymentID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Payments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Payment History

```php
function getPaymentHistory(string $xeroTenantId, string $paymentID): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `paymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Payment |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of HistoryRecords array of 0 to N HistoryRecord

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

```php
    $result = $accountingController->getPaymentHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $paymentID
    );

    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Create Payment History

```php
function createPaymentHistory(string $xeroTenantId, string $paymentID, HistoryRecords $body): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `paymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Payment |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$paymentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createPaymentHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $paymentID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error - API is not able to create HistoryRecord for Payments | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Get Prepayments

```php
function getPrepayments(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?int $page = null,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): Prepayments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 prepayments will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each overpayment |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Prepayments array for all Prepayment

[`Prepayments`](../../doc/models/prepayments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="AUTHORISED"';

$order = 'Reference ASC';

$page = 1;

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getPrepayments(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        $page,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Prepayments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7a9ca0c-6159-4c26-ad2e-715440c50b7d",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552489227595)/",
  "Prepayments": [
    {
      "PrepaymentID": "ce0cddef-cf5a-4e59-b638-f225679115a7",

      "Type": "RECEIVE-PREPAYMENT",
      "Reference": "INV-0011",

        "ContactPersons": [],
        "HasValidationErrors": false
```
