# Create Prepayment Allocations

```php
function createPrepaymentAllocations(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $prepaymentID,
    Allocations $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false
): Allocations
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `prepaymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Prepayment |
| `body` | [`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md) | Body, Required | Allocations with an array of Allocation object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Allocations array of Allocation for all Prepayment

[`Allocations`](../../doc/models/allocations.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$prepaymentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = AllocationsBuilder::init()
    ->allocations(
        [
            AllocationBuilder::init(
                1,
                '2019-01-10',
                InvoiceBuilder::init()
                    ->invoiceID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                    ->lineItems(
                        []
                    )
                    ->build()
            )->build()
        ]
    )->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createPrepaymentAllocations(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $prepaymentID,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'Allocations:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d4758808-d14d-45d5-851a-52787ae5739a",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552522424927)/",
  "Allocations": [
    {
      "Amount": 1.0,
      "Date": "/Date(1552435200000+0000)/",
      "Invoice": {
        "InvoiceID": "c7c37b83-ac95-45ea-88ba-8ad83a5f22fe",
        "Payments": [],
        "CreditNotes": [],
        "Prepayments": [],
        "Overpayments": [],
        "HasErrors": false,
        "IsDiscounted": false,
        "LineItems": [],
        "ValidationErrors": []
      },
      "Prepayment": {
        "PrepaymentID": "ce0cddef-cf5a-4e59-b638-f225679115a7",
        "ID": "ce0cddef-cf5a-4e59-b638-f225679115a7",
        "LineItems": []
      },
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |

| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `prepaymentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a PrePayment |

```php
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createPrepaymentHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $prepaymentID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | Unsupported - return response incorrect exception, API is not able to create HistoryRecord for Expense Claims | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Get Purchase Orders

```php
function getPurchaseOrders(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $status = null,
    ?string $dateFrom = null,
    ?string $dateTo = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?int $page = null
): PurchaseOrders
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `status` | [`?string(Status20Enum)`](../../doc/models/status-20-enum.md) | Query, Optional | Filter by purchase order status |
| `dateFrom` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by purchase order date (e.g. GET https://.../PurchaseOrders?DateFrom=2015-12-01&DateTo=2015-12-31 |
| `dateTo` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by purchase order date (e.g. GET https://.../PurchaseOrders?DateFrom=2015-12-01&DateTo=2015-12-31 |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | To specify a page, append the page parameter to the URL e.g. ?page=1. If there are 100 records in the response you will need to check if there is any more data by fetching the next page e.g ?page=2 and continuing this process until no more results are returned. |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type PurchaseOrder array of all PurchaseOrder

[`PurchaseOrders`](../../doc/models/purchase-orders.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$status = Status20Enum::SUBMITTED;

$dateFrom = '2019-12-01';

$dateTo = '2019-12-31';

$order = 'PurchaseOrderNumber ASC';

$page = 1;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getPurchaseOrders(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $status,
        $dateFrom,
        $dateTo,
        $order,
        $page
    );
    echo 'PurchaseOrders:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update or Create Purchase Orders

```php
function updateOrCreatePurchaseOrders(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    PurchaseOrders $body,
    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false
): PurchaseOrders
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`PurchaseOrders`](../../doc/models/purchase-orders.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type PurchaseOrder array for specified PurchaseOrder

[`PurchaseOrders`](../../doc/models/purchase-orders.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = PurchaseOrdersBuilder::init()
    ->purchaseOrders(
        [
            PurchaseOrderBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2019-03-13')
                ->lineItems(
                    [
                        LineItemBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('710')
                            ->description('Foobar')
                            ->quantity(1)
                            ->unitAmount(20)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateOrCreatePurchaseOrders(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'PurchaseOrders:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Create Purchase Orders

```php

    string $xeroTenantId,

    ?bool $summarizeErrors = false
): PurchaseOrders
```

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |

| `body` | [`PurchaseOrders`](../../doc/models/purchase-orders.md) | Body, Required | PurchaseOrders with an array of PurchaseOrder object in body of request |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

```php
    ->purchaseOrders(
        [
            PurchaseOrderBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2019-03-13')
                ->lineItems(
                    [
                        LineItemBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('710')
                            ->description('Foobar')
                            ->quantity(1)
                            ->unitAmount(20)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

    $result = $accountingController->createPurchaseOrders(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
```

# Get Purchase Order Attachment by Id

```php
function getPurchaseOrderAttachmentById(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $purchaseOrderID,
    string $attachmentID,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `purchaseOrderID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Purchase Order object |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Attachment object |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Account as binary data

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$purchaseOrderID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$contentType = 'image/jpg';

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getPurchaseOrderAttachmentById(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $purchaseOrderID,
        $attachmentID,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Create Purchase Order Attachment by File Name

```php
function createPurchaseOrderAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $purchaseOrderID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `purchaseOrderID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Purchase Order object |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the attachment |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array of Attachment

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$purchaseOrderID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.png';

$body = FileWrapper::createFromPath('dummy_file');

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createPurchaseOrderAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $purchaseOrderID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "c728a4a4-179e-4bbd-a2d5-63e7f9ceba92",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1602099934723)/",
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "e58bd37b-e47f-451a-a42c-f946ef229c3e",
      "FileName": "xero-dev.png",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/PurchaseOrders/93369c9b-c481-4e21-aaab-bb19e9a26efe/Attachments/2D.png",
      "MimeType": "image/png",
      "ContentLength": 82529
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

# Create Purchase Order History

```php
function createPurchaseOrderHistory(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $purchaseOrderID,
    HistoryRecords $body
): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `purchaseOrderID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a PurchaseOrder |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$purchaseOrderID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createPurchaseOrderHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $purchaseOrderID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",

    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",

    }
  ]
}
```

# Get Quotes

```php
function getQuotes(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?\DateTime $dateFrom = null,
    ?\DateTime $dateTo = null,
    ?\DateTime $expiryDateFrom = null,
    ?\DateTime $expiryDateTo = null,
    ?string $contactID = null,
    ?string $status = null,
    ?int $page = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?string $quoteNumber = null
): Quotes
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `dateFrom` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes after a particular date |
| `dateTo` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes before a particular date |
| `expiryDateFrom` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes expiring after a particular date |
| `expiryDateTo` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes before a particular date |
| `contactID` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes belonging to a particular contact |
| `status` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter for quotes of a particular Status |
| `page` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. page=1 – Up to 100 Quotes will be returned in a single API call with line items shown for each quote |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `quoteNumber` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by quote number (e.g. GET https://.../Quotes?QuoteNumber=QU-0001) |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type quotes array with all quotes

[`Quotes`](../../doc/models/quotes.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$contactID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$status = 'DRAFT';

$page = 1;

$order = 'Status ASC';

$quoteNumber = 'QU-0001';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getQuotes(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        $contactID,
        $status,
        $page,
        $order,
        $quoteNumber
    );
    echo 'Quotes:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "bb583e7e-9b6b-471e-88da-4cbfcfad7a57",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Adams OAuth2 App",

    {
      "QuoteID": "be59294f-2a9c-4cee-8c64-0f0ddbc1883a",

        "ContactID": "060816db-0ed7-44de-ab58-8fee9316fcd5",
```

# Update or Create Quotes

```php
function updateOrCreateQuotes(string $xeroTenantId, Quotes $body, ?bool $summarizeErrors = false): Quotes
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Quotes`](../../doc/models/quotes.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `summarizeErrors` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | If false return 200 OK and mix of successfully created objects and any with validation errors<br><br>**Default**: `false` |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Quotes array with updated or created Quote

[`Quotes`](../../doc/models/quotes.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = QuotesBuilder::init()
    ->quotes(
        [
            QuoteBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2020-02-01')
                ->lineItems(
                    [
                        LineItemBuilder::init()
                            ->accountCode('12775')
                            ->description('Foobar')
                            ->quantity(1)
                            ->unitAmount(20)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$summarizeErrors = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateOrCreateQuotes(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $summarizeErrors
    );
    echo 'Quotes:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "SummarizeErrors": false,
```

# Update Quote

```php
function updateQuote(string $xeroTenantId, string $quoteID, Quotes $body): Quotes
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `quoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Quote |
| `body` | [`Quotes`](../../doc/models/quotes.md) | Body, Required | - |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Quotes array with updated Quote

[`Quotes`](../../doc/models/quotes.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$quoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = QuotesBuilder::init()
    ->quotes(
        [
            QuoteBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->date('2020-02-01')
                ->reference('I am an update')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateQuote(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $quoteID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Quotes:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "SummarizeErrors": true,
  "Id": "be4f43a7-ef02-497a-96c2-fc0bc047a82a",
```

# Update Quote Attachment by File Name

```php
function updateQuoteAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $quoteID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `quoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for Quote object |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | Name of the attachment |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array of Attachment

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$quoteID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$body = FileWrapper::createFromPath('dummy_file');

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateQuoteAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $quoteID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "3fa85f64-5717-4562-b3fc-2c963f66afa6",
      "FileName": "sample5.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/Quotes/da962997-a8bd-4dff-9616-01cdc199283f/Attachments/sample5.jpg",
```

# Create Quote History

```php
function createQuoteHistory(string $xeroTenantId, string $quoteID, HistoryRecords $body): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `quoteID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for an Quote |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

```php
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createQuoteHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $quoteID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;

    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Receipts

```php
function getReceipts(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $ifModifiedSince = null,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?int $unitdp = null
): Receipts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Receipts array for all Receipt

[`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'Status=="DRAFT"';

$order = 'ReceiptNumber ASC';

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReceipts(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Receipts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "078b2a2c-902f-4154-8739-357ece5982e5",

        "ValidationErrors": [],
        "Warnings": []
```

# Create Receipt

```php
function createReceipt(string $xeroTenantId, Receipts $body, ?int $unitdp = null): Receipts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md) | Body, Required | Receipts with an array of Receipt object in body of request |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Receipts array for newly created Receipt

[`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = ReceiptsBuilder::init()
    ->receipts(
        [
            ReceiptBuilder::init()
                ->contact(
                    ContactBuilder::init()
                        ->contactID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->lineAmountTypes(LineAmountTypesEnum::NOTAX)
                ->status(Status11Enum::DRAFT)
                ->user(
                    UserBuilder::init()
                        ->userID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createReceipt(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Receipts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Get Receipt

```php
function getReceipt(string $xeroTenantId, string $receiptID, ?int $unitdp = null): Receipts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `receiptID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Receipt |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Receipts array for a specified Receipt

[`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$receiptID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReceipt(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $receiptID,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Receipts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update Receipt

```php
function updateReceipt(string $xeroTenantId, string $receiptID, Receipts $body, ?int $unitdp = null): Receipts
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `receiptID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Receipt |
| `body` | [`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md) | Body, Required | - |
| `unitdp` | `?int` | Query, Optional | e.g. unitdp=4 – (Unit Decimal Places) You can opt in to use four decimal places for unit amounts |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Receipts array for updated Receipt

[`Receipts`](../../doc/models/receipts.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$receiptID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = ReceiptsBuilder::init()
    ->receipts(
        [
            ReceiptBuilder::init()
                ->reference('Foobar')
                ->user(
                    UserBuilder::init()
                        ->userID('00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000')
                        ->build()
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$unitdp = 4;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateReceipt(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $receiptID,
        $body,
        $unitdp
    );
    echo 'Receipts:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*


# Get Receipt Attachment by Id

```php
function getReceiptAttachmentById(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $receiptID,
    string $attachmentID,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `receiptID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Receipt |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Receipt as binary data

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$receiptID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$attachmentID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$contentType = 'image/jpg';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReceiptAttachmentById(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $receiptID,
        $attachmentID,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update Receipt Attachment by File Name

```php
function updateReceiptAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $receiptID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `receiptID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Receipt |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | The name of the file being attached to the Receipt |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with updated Attachment for a specified Receipt

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$receiptID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$body = FileWrapper::createFromPath('dummy_file');

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateReceiptAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $receiptID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "aeca1ea8-8fd9-4757-96a6-397dc4957a69",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1552686602761)/",
  "Attachments": [
    {
      "AttachmentID": "e02a84f6-b83a-4983-b3b9-35cd8880c7bc",
      "FileName": "HelloWorld.jpg",
      "Url": "https://api.xero.com/api.xro/2.0/Receipts/a44fd147-af4e-4fe8-a09a-55332df74162/Attachments/HelloWorld.jpg",
      "MimeType": "image/jpg",
      "ContentLength": 2878711
    }
  ]
}
```

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

```php
    $result = $accountingController->getReceiptHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $receiptID

    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Create Receipt History

```php
function createReceiptHistory(string $xeroTenantId, string $receiptID, HistoryRecords $body): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `receiptID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Receipt |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$receiptID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createReceiptHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $receiptID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "d7525479-3392-44c0-bb37-ff4a0b5df5bd",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | Unsupported - return response incorrect exception, API is not able to create HistoryRecord for Receipts | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |


# Get Repeating Invoices

```php
function getRepeatingInvoices(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null
): RepeatingInvoices
```

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Repeating Invoices array for all Repeating Invoice

[`RepeatingInvoices`](../../doc/models/repeating-invoices.md)

```php
        $xeroTenantId,
        $where,
```

# Get Repeating Invoice Attachment by Id

```php
function getRepeatingInvoiceAttachmentById(

    string $repeatingInvoiceID,
    string $attachmentID,
    string $contentType
): string
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `repeatingInvoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Repeating Invoice |
| `attachmentID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Attachment |
| `contentType` | `string` | Header, Required | The mime type of the attachment file you are retrieving i.e image/jpg, application/pdf |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of attachment for Repeating Invoice as binary data

`string`

## Example Usage

```php
    $result = $accountingController->getRepeatingInvoiceAttachmentById(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $repeatingInvoiceID,
        $attachmentID,
        $contentType
    );
    echo 'string:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Update Repeating Invoice Attachment by File Name

```php
function updateRepeatingInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $repeatingInvoiceID,
    string $fileName,
    FileWrapper $body
): Attachments
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `repeatingInvoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Repeating Invoice |
| `fileName` | `string` | Template, Required | The name of the file being attached to a Repeating Invoice |
| `body` | `FileWrapper` | Form, Required | Byte array of file in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.attachments`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Attachments array with specified Attachment for a specified Repeating Invoice

[`Attachments`](../../doc/models/attachments.md)

```php
$fileName = 'xero-dev.jpg';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateRepeatingInvoiceAttachmentByFileName(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $repeatingInvoiceID,
        $fileName,
        $body
    );
    echo 'Attachments:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Create Repeating Invoice History

```php
function createRepeatingInvoiceHistory(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    string $repeatingInvoiceID,
    HistoryRecords $body
): HistoryRecords
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `repeatingInvoiceID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Repeating Invoice |
| `body` | [`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md) | Body, Required | HistoryRecords containing an array of HistoryRecord objects in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.transactions`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type HistoryRecords array of HistoryRecord objects

[`HistoryRecords`](../../doc/models/history-records.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$repeatingInvoiceID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$body = HistoryRecordsBuilder::init()
    ->historyRecords(
        [
            HistoryRecordBuilder::init()
                ->details('Hello World')
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->createRepeatingInvoiceHistory(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $repeatingInvoiceID,
        $body
    );
    echo 'HistoryRecords:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json

  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Xero API Partner",

  "HistoryRecords": [
    {
      "DateUTCString": "2019-02-23T05:23:20",
      "DateUTC": "/Date(1550899400362)/",
      "Details": "Hello World",
      "ValidationErrors": []
    }
  ]
}
```

## Errors

| HTTP Status Code | Error Description | Exception Class |
|  --- | --- | --- |
| 400 | A failed request due to validation error | [`ErrorException`](../../doc/models/error-exception.md) |

# Get Report Balance Sheet

```php
function getReportBalanceSheet(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $date = null,
    ?int $periods = null,
    ?string $timeframe = null,
    ?string $trackingOptionID1 = null,
    ?string $trackingOptionID2 = null,
    ?bool $standardLayout = null,
    ?bool $paymentsOnly = null
): ReportWithRows
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `date` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | The date of the Balance Sheet report |
| `periods` | `?int` | Query, Optional | The number of periods for the Balance Sheet report |
| `timeframe` | [`?string(TimeframeEnum)`](../../doc/models/timeframe-enum.md) | Query, Optional | The period size to compare to (MONTH, QUARTER, YEAR) |
| `trackingOptionID1` | `?string` | Query, Optional | The tracking option 1 for the Balance Sheet report |
| `trackingOptionID2` | `?string` | Query, Optional | The tracking option 2 for the Balance Sheet report |
| `standardLayout` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | The standard layout boolean for the Balance Sheet report |
| `paymentsOnly` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | return a cash basis for the Balance Sheet report |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

[`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$date = DateTimeHelper::fromSimpleDate('2019-11-01');

$periods = 3;

$timeframe = TimeframeEnum::MONTH;

$trackingOptionID1 = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$trackingOptionID2 = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$standardLayout = true;

$paymentsOnly = false;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReportBalanceSheet(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $date,
        $periods,
        $timeframe,
        $trackingOptionID1,
        $trackingOptionID2,
        $standardLayout,
        $paymentsOnly
    );
    echo 'ReportWithRows:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Report Bank Summary

```php
function getReportBankSummary(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $fromDate = null,
    ?\DateTime $toDate = null
): ReportWithRows
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `fromDate` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | The from date for the Bank Summary report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `toDate` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | The to date for the Bank Summary report e.g. 2018-03-31 |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

[`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$fromDate = DateTimeHelper::fromSimpleDate('2019-11-01');

$toDate = DateTimeHelper::fromSimpleDate('2019-11-30');

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReportBankSummary(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $fromDate,
        $toDate
    );
    echo 'ReportWithRows:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "ae58d0ec-9c5c-455f-b96e-690107579257",

  "ProviderName": "Java Public Example",
```

# Get Report Budget Summary

```php
function getReportBudgetSummary(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $date = null,
    ?int $period = null,
    ?int $timeframe = null
): ReportWithRows
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `date` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | The date for the Bank Summary report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `period` | `?int` | Query, Optional | The number of periods to compare (integer between 1 and 12) |
| `timeframe` | `?int` | Query, Optional | The period size to compare to (1=month, 3=quarter, 12=year) |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: success- return a Report with Rows object

[`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$date = DateTimeHelper::fromSimpleDate('2019-03-31');

$period = 2;

$timeframe = 3;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReportBudgetSummary(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $date,
        $period,
        $timeframe
    );
    echo 'ReportWithRows:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

# Get Report Executive Summary

```php
function getReportExecutiveSummary(string $xeroTenantId, ?\DateTime $date = null): ReportWithRows
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `date` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | The date for the Bank Summary report e.g. 2018-03-31 |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

[`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$date = DateTimeHelper::fromSimpleDate('2019-03-31');

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReportExecutiveSummary(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $date
    );
    echo 'ReportWithRows:';

} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Report Profit and Loss

```php
function getReportProfitAndLoss(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $fromDate = null,
    ?\DateTime $toDate = null,
    ?int $periods = null,
    ?string $timeframe = null,
    ?string $trackingCategoryID = null,
    ?string $trackingCategoryID2 = null,
    ?string $trackingOptionID = null,
    ?string $trackingOptionID2 = null,
    ?bool $standardLayout = null,
    ?bool $paymentsOnly = null
): ReportWithRows
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `fromDate` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | The from date for the ProfitAndLoss report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `toDate` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | The to date for the ProfitAndLoss report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `periods` | `?int` | Query, Optional | The number of periods to compare (integer between 1 and 12) |
| `timeframe` | [`?string(TimeframeEnum)`](../../doc/models/timeframe-enum.md) | Query, Optional | The period size to compare to (MONTH, QUARTER, YEAR) |
| `trackingCategoryID` | `?string` | Query, Optional | The trackingCategory 1 for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `trackingCategoryID2` | `?string` | Query, Optional | The trackingCategory 2 for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `trackingOptionID` | `?string` | Query, Optional | The tracking option 1 for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `trackingOptionID2` | `?string` | Query, Optional | The tracking option 2 for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `standardLayout` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | Return the standard layout for the ProfitAndLoss report |
| `paymentsOnly` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | Return cash only basis for the ProfitAndLoss report |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

[`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$fromDate = DateTimeHelper::fromSimpleDate('2019-03-01');

$toDate = DateTimeHelper::fromSimpleDate('2019-03-31');

$periods = 3;

$timeframe = TimeframeEnum::MONTH;

$trackingCategoryID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$trackingCategoryID2 = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$trackingOptionID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$trackingOptionID2 = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$standardLayout = true;

$paymentsOnly = false;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReportProfitAndLoss(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $fromDate,
        $toDate,
        $periods,
        $timeframe,
        $trackingCategoryID,
        $trackingCategoryID2,
        $trackingOptionID,
        $trackingOptionID2,
        $standardLayout,
        $paymentsOnly
    );
    echo 'ReportWithRows:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Get Report Ten Ninety Nine

```php
function getReportTenNinetyNine(string $xeroTenantId, ?string $reportYear = null): Reports
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `reportYear` | `?string` | Query, Optional | The year of the 1099 report |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.tenninetynine.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Reports

[`Reports`](../../doc/models/reports.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$reportYear = '2019';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReportTenNinetyNine(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $reportYear
    );
    echo 'Reports:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Report Trial Balance

```php
function getReportTrialBalance(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?\DateTime $date = null,
    ?bool $paymentsOnly = null
): ReportWithRows
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `date` | `?DateTime` | Query, Optional | The date for the Trial Balance report e.g. 2018-03-31 |
| `paymentsOnly` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | Return cash only basis for the Trial Balance report |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

[`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$date = DateTimeHelper::fromSimpleDate('2019-10-31');

$paymentsOnly = true;

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReportTrialBalance(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $date,
        $paymentsOnly
    );
    echo 'ReportWithRows:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

# Get Report BA Sor GST

```php
function getReportBASorGST(string $xeroTenantId, string $reportID): ReportWithRows
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `reportID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a Report |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.reports.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type ReportWithRows

[`ReportWithRows`](../../doc/models/report-with-rows.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$reportID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getReportBASorGST(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $reportID
    );
    echo 'ReportWithRows:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```


# Post Setup

```php
function postSetup(string $xeroTenantId, Setup $body): ImportSummaryObject
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`Setup`](../../doc/models/setup.md) | Body, Required | Object including an accounts array, a conversion balances array and a conversion date object in body of request |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - returns a summary of the chart of accounts updates

[`ImportSummaryObject`](../../doc/models/import-summary-object.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = SetupBuilder::init()
    ->accounts(
        [
            AccountBuilder::init()
                ->code('200')
                ->name('Sales')
                ->reportingCode('REV.TRA.GOO')
                ->type(AccountTypeEnum::SALES)
                ->build(),
            AccountBuilder::init()
                ->code('400')
                ->name('Advertising')
                ->reportingCode('EXP')
                ->type(AccountTypeEnum::OVERHEADS)
                ->build(),
            AccountBuilder::init()
                ->code('610')
                ->name('Accounts Receivable')
                ->reportingCode('ASS.CUR.REC.TRA')
                ->type(AccountTypeEnum::CURRENT)
                ->build(),
            AccountBuilder::init()
                ->code('800')
                ->name('Accounts Payable')
                ->reportingCode('LIA.CUR.PAY')
                ->type(AccountTypeEnum::CURRLIAB)
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->conversionBalances(
        []
    )
    ->conversionDate(
        ConversionDateBuilder::init()->build()
    )->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->postSetup(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body
    );
    echo 'ImportSummaryObject:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "80dcb65b-4d14-4350-84e6-1438a809244a",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Java Public Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1604457589645)/",
  "ImportSummary": {
    "Accounts": {
      "Total": 17,
      "New": 0,
      "Updated": 8,
      "Deleted": 0,
      "Locked": 0,
      "System": 9,
      "Errored": 0,
      "Present": true,
      "NewOrUpdated": 8
    },
    "Organisation": {
      "Present": false
    }
  }
}
```


# Get Tax Rates

```php
function getTaxRates(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?string $taxType = null
): TaxRates
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `taxType` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by tax type |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type TaxRates array with TaxRates

[`TaxRates`](../../doc/models/tax-rates.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$where = 'Status=="ACTIVE"';

$order = 'Name ASC';

$taxType = 'INPUT';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getTaxRates(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $where,
        $order,
        $taxType
    );
    echo 'TaxRates:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "455d494d-9706-465b-b584-7086ca406b27",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1555086839841)/",
  "TaxRates": [
    {
      "Name": "15% GST on Expenses",
      "TaxType": "INPUT2",
      "ReportTaxType": "INPUT",
      "CanApplyToAssets": true,
      "CanApplyToEquity": true,
      "CanApplyToExpenses": true,
      "CanApplyToLiabilities": true,
      "CanApplyToRevenue": false,
      "DisplayTaxRate": 15.0,
      "EffectiveRate": 15.0,
      "Status": "ACTIVE",
      "TaxComponents": [
        {
          "Name": "GST",
```

# Update Tax Rate

```php
function updateTaxRate(string $xeroTenantId, TaxRates $body): TaxRates
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `body` | [`TaxRates`](../../doc/models/tax-rates.md) | Body, Required | - |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type TaxRates array updated TaxRate

[`TaxRates`](../../doc/models/tax-rates.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$body = TaxRatesBuilder::init()
    ->taxRates(
        [
            TaxRateBuilder::init()
                ->name('State Tax NY')
                ->reportTaxType(ReportTaxTypeEnum::INPUT)
                ->status(Status19Enum::DELETED)
                ->taxComponents(
                    [
                        TaxComponentBuilder::init()
                            ->name('State Tax')
                            ->rate(2.25)
                            ->build()
                    ]
                )
                ->build()
        ]
    )
    ->build();

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->updateTaxRate(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $body
    );
    echo 'TaxRates:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ErrorException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught ErrorException:', $exp;
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "12f4c453-2e25-41aa-a52f-6faaf6c05832",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1555086839658)/",
  "TaxRates": [
    {
      "Name": "SDKTax29067",
      "TaxType": "TAX002",
      "ReportTaxType": "INPUT",
      "CanApplyToAssets": true,
      "CanApplyToEquity": true,
      "CanApplyToExpenses": true,
      "CanApplyToLiabilities": true,
      "CanApplyToRevenue": false,
      "DisplayTaxRate": 2.25,
      "EffectiveRate": 2.25,
      "Status": "DELETED",
      "TaxComponents": [
        {
          "Name": "State Tax",
          "Rate": 2.25,
          "IsCompound": false,
          "IsNonRecoverable": false
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

# Get Tracking Categories

```php
function getTrackingCategories(
    string $xeroTenantId,
    ?string $where = null,
    ?string $order = null,
    ?bool $includeArchived = null
): TrackingCategories
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |
| `includeArchived` | `?bool` | Query, Optional | e.g. includeArchived=true - Categories and options with a status of ARCHIVED will be included in the response |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type TrackingCategories array of TrackingCategory

[`TrackingCategories`](../../doc/models/tracking-categories.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$where = 'Status=="ACTIVE"';

$order = 'Name ASC';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getTrackingCategories(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $where,
        $order
    );
    echo 'TrackingCategories:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "cec55068-8061-48e5-ac83-c77e7c54cf3d",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1555085855047)/",
  "TrackingCategories": [
    {
      "Name": "BarFoo",
      "Status": "ACTIVE",
      "TrackingCategoryID": "22f10184-0deb-44ae-a312-b1f6ea70e51f",
      "Options": []
    },
    {
      "Name": "HelloWorld",
      "Status": "ACTIVE",
      "TrackingCategoryID": "0c9fce3e-a111-4d99-803a-62cf3f40e633",
      "Options": []
    }
  ]
}
```


## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `ifModifiedSince` | `?DateTime` | Header, Optional | Only records created or modified since this timestamp will be returned |
| `where` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Filter by an any element |
| `order` | `?string` | Query, Optional | Order by an any element |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Users array of all User

[`Users`](../../doc/models/users.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$ifModifiedSince = DateTimeHelper::fromRfc3339DateTime('02/06/2020 20:17:43');

$where = 'IsSubscriber==true';

$order = 'LastName ASC';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getUsers(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $ifModifiedSince,
        $where,
        $order
    );
    echo 'Users:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "17932a4e-4948-4d50-8672-4ef0e1dd90c5",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1553880796393)/",
  "Users": [
    {
      "UserID": "3c37ef1d-cd49-4589-9787-3c418ed8b6ac",
      "EmailAddress": "test@email.com",
      "FirstName": "Test",
      "LastName": "Xero",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1508523261613+0000)/",
      "IsSubscriber": false,
      "OrganisationRole": "FINANCIALADVISER"
    },
    {
      "UserID": "d1164823-0ac1-41ad-987b-b4e30fe0b273",
      "EmailAddress": "api@xero.com",
      "FirstName": "API ",
      "LastName": "Team",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1511957179217+0000)/",
      "IsSubscriber": true,
      "OrganisationRole": "FINANCIALADVISER"
    }
  ]

```


# Get User

```php
function getUser(string $xeroTenantId, string $userID): Users
```

## Authentication

This endpoint requires [OAuth2](../../doc/auth/oauth-2-authorization-code-grant.md)

## Parameters

| Parameter | Type | Tags | Description |
|  --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `xeroTenantId` | `string` | Header, Required | Xero identifier for Tenant |
| `userID` | `string` | Template, Required | Unique identifier for a User |

## Requires scope

### OAuth2

`accounting.settings.read`

## Response Type

**200**: Success - return response of type Users array of specified User

[`Users`](../../doc/models/users.md)

## Example Usage

```php
$xeroTenantId = 'YOUR_XERO_TENANT_ID';

$userID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000';

$accountingController = $client->getAccountingController();

try {
    $result = $accountingController->getUser(
        $xeroTenantId,
        $userID
    );
    echo 'Users:';
    var_dump($result);
} catch (ApiException $exp) {
    echo 'Caught:', $exp;
}
```

## Example Response *(as JSON)*

```json
{
  "Id": "51250ce8-1b35-4ba4-b404-dc94ff75bd87",
  "Status": "OK",
  "ProviderName": "Provider Name Example",
  "DateTimeUTC": "/Date(1553880796732)/",
  "Users": [
    {
      "UserID": "3c37ef1d-cd49-4589-9787-3c418ed8b6ac",
      "EmailAddress": "test@email.com",
      "FirstName": "Test",
      "LastName": "Xero",
      "UpdatedDateUTC": "/Date(1508523261613+0000)/",
      "IsSubscriber": false,
      "OrganisationRole": "FINANCIALADVISER"
    }
  ]
}
```
